<article id="post-2189849" class="post-2189849 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-news category-wildlife tag-bears tag-brown-bears tag-european-brown-bear tag-marsican-brown-bear tag-polar-bears">
	<div data-BgLz="1" class="blog-item-wrap">
				<a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/living-near-humans-italian-bears-evolved-to-be-less-aggressive/" title="Living Near Humans, Italian Bears Evolved to Be Less Aggressive" >
				<img post-id="2189849" fifu-featured="1" width="750" data-class="LazyLoad" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='1200'%20height='500'%3E%3Crect%20width='100%25'%20height='100%25'%20opacity='0'/%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://i0.wp.com/assets.nautil.us/sites/3/nautilus/X9hqGxNj-Reese_HERO.png?q=65&amp;auto=format&amp;w=1200&amp;w=750&amp;resize=750,0&amp;ssl=1" class="single-featured wp-post-image" alt="Living Near Humans, Italian Bears Evolved to Be Less Aggressive" title="Living Near Humans, Italian Bears Evolved to Be Less Aggressive" title="Living Near Humans, Italian Bears Evolved to Be Less Aggressive" decoding="async" />			</a>
		<div data-BgLz="1" class="post-inner-content">
			<header class="entry-header page-header">

				<h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/living-near-humans-italian-bears-evolved-to-be-less-aggressive/" rel="bookmark">Living Near Humans, Italian Bears Evolved to Be Less Aggressive</a></h2>

								<div data-BgLz="1" class="entry-meta">
					<span class="posted-on"><i class="fa fa-calendar-alt"></i> <a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/living-near-humans-italian-bears-evolved-to-be-less-aggressive/" rel="bookmark"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-24T06:00:40+01:00">February 24, 2026</time><time class="updated" datetime="2025-12-18T14:52:02+01:00">December 18, 2025</time></a></span><span class="byline"> <i class="fa fa-user"></i> <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/author/supertrooper/">Supertrooper</a></span></span>				<span class="comments-link"><i class="fa fa-comment-o"></i><a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/living-near-humans-italian-bears-evolved-to-be-less-aggressive/#comments">1 Comment</a></span>

							</header><!-- .entry-header -->

						<div data-BgLz="1" class="entry-content">

				<p>Brown bears living near villages in central Italy have evolved to be less aggressive, according to a new study, the latest to show how humans are shaping the evolution of wildlife. Marsican brown bears have been isolated from other European brown bears since the Roman era, cut off by expanding farms and cities. Over centuries [&hellip;]</p>

<article id="post-2189746" class="post-2189746 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-news category-petitions category-wildlife tag-marine-animals tag-marine-mammals tag-orca tag-seaquarium tag-seaworld">
	<div data-BgLz="1" class="blog-item-wrap">
				<a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/petition-close-seaworld-and-release-all-captive-marine-animals-to-sanctuaries/" title="Petition: Close SeaWorld and Release All Captive Marine Animals to Sanctuaries" >
				<img post-id="2189746" fifu-featured="1" width="750" data-class="LazyLoad" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='1200'%20height='500'%3E%3Crect%20width='100%25'%20height='100%25'%20opacity='0'/%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://i3.wp.com/dingo.care2.com/pictures/petition_images/petition/657/955000-1763650097-wide_facebook.jpg?w=750&amp;resize=750,0&amp;ssl=1" class="single-featured wp-post-image" alt="Petition: Close SeaWorld and Release All Captive Marine Animals to Sanctuaries" title="Petition: Close SeaWorld and Release All Captive Marine Animals to Sanctuaries" title="Petition: Close SeaWorld and Release All Captive Marine Animals to Sanctuaries" decoding="async" />			</a>
		<div data-BgLz="1" class="post-inner-content">
			<header class="entry-header page-header">

				<h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/petition-close-seaworld-and-release-all-captive-marine-animals-to-sanctuaries/" rel="bookmark">Petition: Close SeaWorld and Release All Captive Marine Animals to Sanctuaries</a></h2>

								<div data-BgLz="1" class="entry-meta">
					<span class="posted-on"><i class="fa fa-calendar-alt"></i> <a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/petition-close-seaworld-and-release-all-captive-marine-animals-to-sanctuaries/" rel="bookmark"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-23T18:00:28+01:00">February 23, 2026</time><time class="updated" datetime="2025-12-18T14:52:02+01:00">December 18, 2025</time></a></span><span class="byline"> <i class="fa fa-user"></i> <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/author/supertrooper/">Supertrooper</a></span></span>				<span class="comments-link"><i class="fa fa-comment-o"></i><a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/petition-close-seaworld-and-release-all-captive-marine-animals-to-sanctuaries/#comments">1 Comment</a></span>

							</header><!-- .entry-header -->

						<div data-BgLz="1" class="entry-content">

				<p>In a massive victory for animal rights, the Miami Seaquarium has closed its doors for good! The &#8220;marine theme park,&#8221; which operated for 70 years, spent decades profiting off of the misery of captive animals. We must keep the momentum up! It&#8217;s time for SeaWorld to close all locations and move every single captive animal [&hellip;]</p>

	<div data-BgLz="1" class="blog-item-wrap">
				<a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/peregrine-falcons-retain-trade-protections-despite-downlisting-bid-by-canada-and-us/" title="Peregrine falcons retain trade protections, despite downlisting bid by Canada and US" >
				<img post-id="2189744" fifu-featured="1" width="750" data-class="LazyLoad" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='1200'%20height='500'%3E%3Crect%20width='100%25'%20height='100%25'%20opacity='0'/%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://i1.wp.com/imgs.mongabay.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/20/2025/12/03195425/pf-1200x800.jpg?w=750&amp;resize=750,0&amp;ssl=1" class="single-featured wp-post-image" alt="Peregrine falcons retain trade protections, despite downlisting bid by Canada and US" title="Peregrine falcons retain trade protections, despite downlisting bid by Canada and US" title="Peregrine falcons retain trade protections, despite downlisting bid by Canada and US" decoding="async" />			</a>
		<div data-BgLz="1" class="post-inner-content">
			<header class="entry-header page-header">

				<h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/peregrine-falcons-retain-trade-protections-despite-downlisting-bid-by-canada-and-us/" rel="bookmark">Peregrine falcons retain trade protections, despite downlisting bid by Canada and US</a></h2>

								<div data-BgLz="1" class="entry-meta">
					<span class="posted-on"><i class="fa fa-calendar-alt"></i> <a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/peregrine-falcons-retain-trade-protections-despite-downlisting-bid-by-canada-and-us/" rel="bookmark"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-22T18:00:00+01:00">February 22, 2026</time><time class="updated" datetime="2025-12-18T14:52:03+01:00">December 18, 2025</time></a></span><span class="byline"> <i class="fa fa-user"></i> <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/author/supertrooper/">Supertrooper</a></span></span>				<span class="comments-link"><i class="fa fa-comment-o"></i><a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/peregrine-falcons-retain-trade-protections-despite-downlisting-bid-by-canada-and-us/#comments">2 Comments</a></span>

							</header><!-- .entry-header -->

						<div data-BgLz="1" class="entry-content">

				<p>The U.S. and Canada have failed in their bid to loosen restrictions on the international trade in peregrine falcons, with delegates to CITES, the global wildlife trade convention, voting against it at an summit underway in Samarkand, Uzbekistan. The two countries had submitted a joint proposal to move peregrine falcons (Falco peregrinus) from CITES Appendix [&hellip;]</p>

				<h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/police-investigate-after-white-tailed-eagles-go-missing-across-uk/" rel="bookmark">Police investigate after white-tailed eagles go missing across UK</a></h2>

								<div data-BgLz="1" class="entry-meta">
					<span class="posted-on"><i class="fa fa-calendar-alt"></i> <a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/police-investigate-after-white-tailed-eagles-go-missing-across-uk/" rel="bookmark"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-21T06:00:24+01:00">February 21, 2026</time><time class="updated" datetime="2025-12-18T14:52:03+01:00">December 18, 2025</time></a></span><span class="byline"> <i class="fa fa-user"></i> <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/author/supertrooper/">Supertrooper</a></span></span>				<span class="comments-link"><i class="fa fa-comment-o"></i><a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/police-investigate-after-white-tailed-eagles-go-missing-across-uk/#comments">3 Comments</a></span>
				
				
				</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
							</header><!-- .entry-header -->

						<div data-BgLz="1" class="entry-content">

				<p>One of the first white-tailed eagles to fledge in England for hundreds of years has vanished in suspicious circumstances, alongside two more “devastating” disappearances of the reintroduced raptor. Police are appealing for public help as they investigate the disappearances, which are a setback to the bird’s successful reintroduction. Their disappearance is being investigated by several [&hellip;]</p>

	<div data-BgLz="1" class="blog-item-wrap">
				<a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/saving-critical-winter-habitat-for-monarch-butterflies-may-depend-on-buy-in-from-their-human-neighbors/" title="Saving critical winter habitat for monarch butterflies may depend on buy-in from their human neighbors" >
				<img post-id="2189740" fifu-featured="1" width="750" data-class="LazyLoad" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='1200'%20height='500'%3E%3Crect%20width='100%25'%20height='100%25'%20opacity='0'/%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://i2.wp.com/imgs.mongabay.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/20/2025/12/03133322/Photo4_Monarch-butterfly-resting-on-a-plant-1200x800.jpg?w=750&amp;resize=750,0&amp;ssl=1" class="single-featured wp-post-image" alt="Saving critical winter habitat for monarch butterflies may depend on buy-in from their human neighbors" title="Saving critical winter habitat for monarch butterflies may depend on buy-in from their human neighbors" title="Saving critical winter habitat for monarch butterflies may depend on buy-in from their human neighbors" decoding="async" />			</a>
		<div data-BgLz="1" class="post-inner-content">
			<header class="entry-header page-header">

				<h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/saving-critical-winter-habitat-for-monarch-butterflies-may-depend-on-buy-in-from-their-human-neighbors/" rel="bookmark">Saving critical winter habitat for monarch butterflies may depend on buy-in from their human neighbors</a></h2>

								<div data-BgLz="1" class="entry-meta">
					<span class="posted-on"><i class="fa fa-calendar-alt"></i> <a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/saving-critical-winter-habitat-for-monarch-butterflies-may-depend-on-buy-in-from-their-human-neighbors/" rel="bookmark"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2026-02-20T18:00:44+01:00">February 20, 2026</time><time class="updated" datetime="2025-12-18T14:52:04+01:00">December 18, 2025</time></a></span><span class="byline"> <i class="fa fa-user"></i> <span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/author/supertrooper/">Supertrooper</a></span></span>				<span class="comments-link"><i class="fa fa-comment-o"></i><a href="https://focusingonwildlife.com/news/saving-critical-winter-habitat-for-monarch-butterflies-may-depend-on-buy-in-from-their-human-neighbors/#comments">3 Comments</a></span>
				
				
				</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
							</header><!-- .entry-header -->

						<div data-BgLz="1" class="entry-content">

				<p>The monarch butterfly (Danaus plexippus) population has plummeted by 80% to 95% since the 1990s, depending on the region and monitoring method. A major cause of the species’ decline is deforestation in central Mexico, where eastern monarchs spend the colder winter months of their annual migration from Canada and the northern United States. Since 1980, [&hellip;]</p>
